""SELECT t.\"FarmId\", (
    SELECT f.\"Name\"
    FROM \"TillagePrograms\" AS t0
    INNER JOIN \"Farms\" AS f ON t0.\"FarmId\" = f.\"Id\"
    WHERE t0.\"FarmId\" = @__farmId_0 AND t0.\"IsActive\" AND t.\"FarmId\" = t0.\"FarmId\"
    LIMIT 1) AS \"FarmName\", COALESCE(sum(t.\"TotalHectares\"), 0) AS \"TotalPlanned\", COALESCE(sum(t.\"TilledHectares\"), 0) AS \"TotalTilled\", COALESCE(sum((
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM \"TillageServices\" AS t1
    WHERE t.\"Id\" = t1.\"TillageProgramId\")), 0)::int AS \"TotalServices\", COALESCE(sum((
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM \"TillageServices\" AS t2
    WHERE t.\"Id\" = t2.\"TillageProgramId\" AND t2.\"IsCompleted\")), 0)::int AS \"CompletedServices\", COALESCE(sum((
    SELECT COALESCE(sum(COALESCE(t3.\"ServiceCost\", 0.0)), 0.0)
    FROM \"TillageServices\" AS t3
    WHERE t.\"Id\" = t3.\"TillageProgramId\")), 0.0) AS \"TotalRevenue\"
FROM \"TillagePrograms\" AS t
WHERE t.\"FarmId\" = @__farmId_0 AND t.\"IsActive\"
GROUP BY t.\"FarmId\"
LIMIT 1"
